        <div _ngcontent-c88="" class="description half"> 
         <h2 _ngcontent-c88="">Why Take This Nanodegree Program?</h2> 
         <!---->
         <p _ngcontent-c88="" class="mb-0" innerhtml="Robots are enhancing productivity, safety, and efficiency across whole industries&amp;#8212;from manufacturing and healthcare to agriculture, construction, and transportation. In the process, we are being freed to pursue more creative, ambitious, and intellectual achievements. Incredible new opportunities are emerging, but they require specialized skills. This program will teach you exactly what you need to know to join the new generation of engineers who are changing our world for the better by leveraging the power of robotics to extend our capabilities in innovative and beneficial new ways.">Robots are enhancing productivity, safety, and efficiency across whole industriesfrom manufacturing and healthcare to agriculture, construction, and transportation. In the process, we are being freed to pursue more creative, ambitious, and intellectual achievements. Incredible new opportunities are emerging, but they require specialized skills. This program will teach you exactly what you need to know to join the new generation of engineers who are changing our world for the better by leveraging the power of robotics to extend our capabilities in innovative and beneficial new ways.</p> 
         <br _ngcontent-c88="">

     <section _ngcontent-c82=""> 
      <!---->
      <ir-degree-syllabus _ngcontent-c82="" _nghost-c105="">
       <div _ngcontent-c105="" class="contain no-padding-top no-padding-bottom"> 
        <h4 _ngcontent-c105="" class="h2 section-header" style="display: inline-block; text-transform: none;">What You Will Learn</h4> 
        <!----> 
       </div> 
       <!----> 
       <!---->
       <!----> 
       <section _ngcontent-c105="" class="nd-syllabus-term__cards"> 
        <div _ngcontent-c105="" class="cards_contain contain contain--none"> 
         <!---->
         <a _ngcontent-c105="" class="button--secondary lg syllabus-download-button" target="_blank" href="https://medium.com/udacity/robotics-nanodegree-program-syllabus-term-one-in-depth-d7a802b04c98">Download Syllabus</a> 
         <div _ngcontent-c105="" class="nd-syllabus-term__card"> 
          <section _ngcontent-c105="" class="nd-syllabus-term__header"> 
           <div _ngcontent-c105="" class="nd-syllabus-term__header__image" irdeferbgimage="" style=""></div> 
           <div _ngcontent-c105="" class="nd-syllabus-term__header__content"> 
            <!---->
            <h6 _ngcontent-c105="">TERM 1</h6> 
            <h2 _ngcontent-c105="" class="h3">ROS Essentials, Perception &amp; Control</h2> 
            <p _ngcontent-c105="" class="small hidden-md-down">Break into the world of Robotics with a practical, system focused approach to building robots using the ROS framework. Leverage modern machine learning and classical mechanics to implement the key robot functions of perception and control.</p> 
            <p _ngcontent-c105="" class="small hidden-lg-up">Apply modern machine learning and classical mechanics to the key robot functions of perception and control using ROS.</p> 
            <!----> 
            <div _ngcontent-c105="" class="nd-syllabus-term__header__content--details"> 
             <p _ngcontent-c105="" class="nd-syllabus-term__toggle text-only"> 
              <!----><span _ngcontent-c105="">See details</span> 
              <!----> </p> 
             <p _ngcontent-c105="" class="x-small gray-medium hidden-md-down">3 months to complete </p> 
            </div> 
           </div> 
          </section> 
          <section _ngcontent-c105="" class="nd-syllabus-term__main collapse" style="height:0;" aria-expanded="false" aria-hidden="true"> 
           <div _ngcontent-c105="" class="nd-syllabus-term__main__content"> 
            <!---->
            <!----> 
            <h6 _ngcontent-c105="" class="mb-half">Prerequisite Knowledge</h6> 
            <p _ngcontent-c105="" class="small mb-2"> Knowledge of foundational calculus, linear algebra, probability, statistics, basic physics and intermediate Python is required. Existing experience with intermediate C++ and knowledge of machine learning techniques is recommended but not required. 
             <!---->
             <!----> 
             <!----><a _ngcontent-c105="">See detailed requirements.</a> </p> 
            <section _ngcontent-c105="" class="nd-syllabus-term__main__content--parts"> 
             <!---->
             <!----> 
             <!----> 
             <ul _ngcontent-c105=""> 
              <!---->
              <li _ngcontent-c105=""> 
               <div _ngcontent-c105="" class="part"> 
                <!---->
                <h4 _ngcontent-c105="" class="h5 mb-half">Introduction To Robotics</h4> 
                <p _ngcontent-c105="" class="small mb-half">Discover the world of Robotics and get oriented with the core elements that comprise a Nanodegree program. Then put on your NASA thinking cap and getting a sense of how a space rover can perceive, make decisions, and take action to successfully accomplish its mission.</p> 
                <!---->
                <!----> 
                <!---->
                <a _ngcontent-c105="" class="part__project text-only"> <img _ngcontent-c105="" class="icon-middle" src="/assets/iridium/images/nanodegree-overview/shared/degree-syllabus/icon-project.svg"> <span _ngcontent-c105="">Search and Sample Return</span> </a> 
               </div> </li>
              <li _ngcontent-c105=""> 
               <div _ngcontent-c105="" class="part"> 
                <!---->
                <h4 _ngcontent-c105="" class="h5 mb-half">ROS Essentials</h4> 
                <p _ngcontent-c105="" class="small mb-half">Learn the programmatic fundamentals of ROS, the Robot Operating System framework and start writing code thats capable of controlling a real robot.</p> 
                <!----> 
               </div> </li>
              <li _ngcontent-c105=""> 
               <div _ngcontent-c105="" class="part"> 
                <!---->
                <h4 _ngcontent-c105="" class="h5 mb-half">Kinematics</h4> 
                <p _ngcontent-c105="" class="small mb-half">Dive into the world of Kinematics, a branch of mechanics that defines the mathematical and scientific backbone for describing how a robot moves. Youll program a robotic arm with six degrees of freedom to deftly locate an object, pick it up, and then place it in a new destination.</p> 
                <!---->
                <!----> 
                <!---->
                <a _ngcontent-c105="" class="part__project text-only"> <img _ngcontent-c105="" class="icon-middle" src="/assets/iridium/images/nanodegree-overview/shared/degree-syllabus/icon-project.svg"> <span _ngcontent-c105="">Robotic Arm: Pick and Place</span> </a> 
               </div> </li>
              <li _ngcontent-c105=""> 
               <div _ngcontent-c105="" class="part"> 
                <!---->
                <h4 _ngcontent-c105="" class="h5 mb-half">Perception</h4> 
                <p _ngcontent-c105="" class="small mb-half">Explore object recognition, segmentation, and how to process depth data from camera sensors to help a robot better understand and navigate its world.</p> 
                <!---->
                <!----> 
                <!---->
                <a _ngcontent-c105="" class="part__project text-only"> <img _ngcontent-c105="" class="icon-middle" src="/assets/iridium/images/nanodegree-overview/shared/degree-syllabus/icon-project.svg"> <span _ngcontent-c105="">Robotic Arm: Perception</span> </a> 
               </div> </li>
              <li _ngcontent-c105=""> 
               <div _ngcontent-c105="" class="part"> 
                <!---->
                <h4 _ngcontent-c105="" class="h5 mb-half">Controls</h4> 
                <p _ngcontent-c105="" class="small mb-half">Learn the fundamentals of some of the most widely used control algorithms so that you can implement an efficient solution of your own. Youll explore this realm by programming a drone flight controller.</p> 
                <!----> 
               </div> </li>
              <li _ngcontent-c105=""> 
               <div _ngcontent-c105="" class="part"> 
                <!---->
                <h4 _ngcontent-c105="" class="h5 mb-half">Deep Learning For Robotics</h4> 
                <p _ngcontent-c105="" class="small mb-half">Learn how to apply deep neural networks to perception and control tasks.</p> 
                <!---->
                <!----> 
                <!---->
                <a _ngcontent-c105="" class="part__project text-only"> <img _ngcontent-c105="" class="icon-middle" src="/assets/iridium/images/nanodegree-overview/shared/degree-syllabus/icon-project.svg"> <span _ngcontent-c105="">Follow Me</span> </a> 
               </div> </li> 
             </ul> 
            </section> 
           </div> 
           <!---->
           <div _ngcontent-c105="" class="nd-syllabus-term__main__aside"> 
            <aside _ngcontent-c105=""> 
             <img _ngcontent-c105="" src="/assets/iridium/images/nanodegree-overview/shared/degree-syllabus/icon-prepare.svg"> 
             <h6 _ngcontent-c105="" class="mb-half">Need to prepare?</h6> 
             <p _ngcontent-c105="" class="small" innerhtml="Please refer to the list of helpful resources in our <a href=&quot;/robotics/faq#prerequisites&quot;>FAQ</a>.">Please refer to the list of helpful resources in our <a href="/robotics/faq#prerequisites">FAQ</a>.</p> 
            </aside> 
           </div> 
          </section> 
         </div> 
        </div> 
       </section> 
       <!---->

          <section _ngcontent-c105="" class="nd-syllabus-term__header">

            <p _ngcontent-c105="" class="small hidden-md-down">The second Term of the Robotics Nanodegree program is under construction. We'll update this soon.</p> 
            <p _ngcontent-c105="" class="small hidden-lg-up">The second Term of the Robotics Nanodegree program is under construction. We'll update this soon.</p>

           <h4 _ngcontent-c105="" class="h2 text-center">Prerequisites and Requirements</h4>

            <p>To succeed in this program, you need to have significant experience with:</p>

             <li>Calculus and Linear Algebra</li>
             <li>Statistics and Probability</li>
             <li>Intermediate Python</li>

             <li>Machine Learning</li>

         <div _ngcontent-c37="" class="faq__header"> 
          <h4 _ngcontent-c37="" class="h2">
           <!---->FAQ</h4> 
          <!----> 
          <!----> 
          <!---->
          <div _ngcontent-c37="" class="faq__header--button"> 
           <a _ngcontent-c37="" class="button--secondary" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank" href="https://www.udacity.com/robotics/faq">View All FAQ</a> 
          </div> 
         </div> 
         <div _ngcontent-c37="" class="more fade"> 
          <div _ngcontent-c37=""> 
           <!---->
           <ul _ngcontent-c37="" class="faq__list"> 
            <!----> 
            <!---->
            <li _ngcontent-c37=""> <h6 _ngcontent-c37="" class="h4">Why should I enroll in the Robotics Nanodegree program?</h6> 
             <!---->
             <div _ngcontent-c37="" class="answer-content" innerhtml="<p>The field of robotics is growing fast and the demand for engineers with the right skills far exceeds the current supply. This program represents a unique opportunity to develop these in-demand skills. We are partnering with the best companies in the field of robotics to offer in-depth curriculum, expert instructors, and exclusive hiring opportunities. You will come out of this program having completed several hand-on robotics projects, both in simulation and on real hardware, that will serve as portfolio pieces that demonstrate the skills you&amp;#8217;ve acquired. This is an ideal program for anyone seeking to launch or advance a career in this incredible field.</p>">
              <p>The field of robotics is growing fast and the demand for engineers with the right skills far exceeds the current supply. This program represents a unique opportunity to develop these in-demand skills. We are partnering with the best companies in the field of robotics to offer in-depth curriculum, expert instructors, and exclusive hiring opportunities. You will come out of this program having completed several hand-on robotics projects, both in simulation and on real hardware, that will serve as portfolio pieces that demonstrate the skills youve acquired. This is an ideal program for anyone seeking to launch or advance a career in this incredible field.</p>
             </div> </li>
            <li _ngcontent-c37=""> <h6 _ngcontent-c37="" class="h4">What kinds of topics will the program cover?</h6> 
             <!---->
             <div _ngcontent-c37="" class="answer-content" innerhtml="<p>The program will cover topics including perception, localization, path planning, and control. Computer Vision and machine / deep learning techniques for robot perception will also be covered, as well as the Robot Operating System (ROS) and an introduction to robotic hardware systems.</p>">
              <p>The program will cover topics including perception, localization, path planning, and control. Computer Vision and machine / deep learning techniques for robot perception will also be covered, as well as the Robot Operating System (ROS) and an introduction to robotic hardware systems.</p>
             </div> </li>
            <li _ngcontent-c37=""> <h6 _ngcontent-c37="" class="h4">How is the Robotics Nanodegree program different from your Machine Learning Engineer Nanodegree program or your Self-Driving Car Engineer Nanodegree program?</h6> 
             <!---->
             <div _ngcontent-c37="" class="answer-content" innerhtml="<p>The Machine Learning Engineer Nanodegree program is the most general of the three programs. It offers a great foundation, and is an excellent choice for anyone pursuing a career in a field where machine learning techniques are used. However, the curriculum is not as advanced as the other two programs, and it does not specialize to the same extent.</p><p>The Machine Learning Engineer program is not an official prerequisite for either the Self-Driving Car or Robotics programs, though it may be beneficial to some students to complete this program first, depending on your existing knowledge and experience.</p><p>The Robotics program provides an introduction to various aspects of robotics including perception, localization, path planning, and control, as well as the Robot Operating System (ROS). All of the techniques required to complete the projects in the Robotics program (including machine learning) are taught as part of the program.</p><p>The Self-Driving Car Nanodegree is a specialized robotics program; it uses robotics concepts and applies them to a self-driving car. If you are interested in robotics in general beyond the field of self-driving cars, then the Robotics Nanodegree Program is for you.</p>">
              <p>The Machine Learning Engineer Nanodegree program is the most general of the three programs. It offers a great foundation, and is an excellent choice for anyone pursuing a career in a field where machine learning techniques are used. However, the curriculum is not as advanced as the other two programs, and it does not specialize to the same extent.</p>
              <p>The Machine Learning Engineer program is not an official prerequisite for either the Self-Driving Car or Robotics programs, though it may be beneficial to some students to complete this program first, depending on your existing knowledge and experience.</p>
              <p>The Robotics program provides an introduction to various aspects of robotics including perception, localization, path planning, and control, as well as the Robot Operating System (ROS). All of the techniques required to complete the projects in the Robotics program (including machine learning) are taught as part of the program.</p>
              <p>The Self-Driving Car Nanodegree is a specialized robotics program; it uses robotics concepts and applies them to a self-driving car. If you are interested in robotics in general beyond the field of self-driving cars, then the Robotics Nanodegree Program is for you.</p>
             </div> </li>
            <li _ngcontent-c37=""> <h6 _ngcontent-c37="" class="h4">How are you developing the curriculum and who are your partners?</h6> 
             <!---->
             <div _ngcontent-c37="" class="answer-content" innerhtml="<p>Udacity is developing the curriculum for the Robotics Nanodegree program in close partnership with <a href=&quot;http://www.electricmovement.com/&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;>Electric Movement</a>, a cutting-edge robotics engineering company in the Bay Area.  Electric Movement is a pioneer in the space of rapid prototyping and development of robotics solutions for companies of all sizes.  Their work touches every aspect of robotics, from conceptual design to production. They are an ideal partner to help us deliver a comprehensive and world-class experience for our students.</p><p>Udacity is also building content in partnership with <a href=&quot;https://www.megabots.com/&quot;>Megabots</a>, a company focused on &amp;#8220;leveraging deep engineering expertise in the rapidly advancing field of hydraulic robotics in order to empower an entire generation of creators to actually build the robots of science fiction for the first time.&amp;#8221;</p>">
              <p>Udacity is developing the curriculum for the Robotics Nanodegree program in close partnership with <a href="http://www.electricmovement.com/" target="_blank">Electric Movement</a>, a cutting-edge robotics engineering company in the Bay Area. Electric Movement is a pioneer in the space of rapid prototyping and development of robotics solutions for companies of all sizes. Their work touches every aspect of robotics, from conceptual design to production. They are an ideal partner to help us deliver a comprehensive and world-class experience for our students.</p>
              <p>Udacity is also building content in partnership with <a href="https://www.megabots.com/">Megabots</a>, a company focused on leveraging deep engineering expertise in the rapidly advancing field of hydraulic robotics in order to empower an entire generation of creators to actually build the robots of science fiction for the first time.</p>
             </div> </li>
            <li _ngcontent-c37=""> <h6 _ngcontent-c37="" class="h4">Does this program have hiring partnerships associated with it?</h6> 
             <!---->
             <div _ngcontent-c37="" class="answer-content" innerhtml="<p>Yes! We are thrilled to have as hiring partners these leading-edge companies that will fast track graduates for job consideration at their companies: Lockheed Martin, Uber ATG, Kuka, Bosch, Electric Movement, MegaBots, iRobot, and X, Alphabet&amp;#8217;s Moonshot Factory.</p>">
              <p>Yes! We are thrilled to have as hiring partners these leading-edge companies that will fast track graduates for job consideration at their companies: Lockheed Martin, Uber ATG, Kuka, Bosch, Electric Movement, MegaBots, iRobot, and X, Alphabets Moonshot Factory.</p>
             </div> </li>
            <li _ngcontent-c37=""> <h6 _ngcontent-c37="" class="h4">What jobs will this program prepare me for?</h6> 
             <!---->
             <div _ngcontent-c37="" class="answer-content" innerhtml="<p>Our goal with this program is to equip you with the most valuable skills in this field; the skills top companies are looking for as they search for the next generation of robotics talent. Enter the search terms &amp;#8220;Robotics Engineer&amp;#8221; in <a href=&quot;https://www.glassdoor.com/index.htm&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;>Glassdoor</a>, <a href=&quot;https://www.indeed.com/&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;>Indeed</a>, or any other major job search engine, and you&amp;#8217;ll find thousands of openings all over the world in a diversity of industries.  To ensure you&amp;#8217;re well-prepared to meet this demand, this program will focus on the software behind robotics systems, while also providing you the opportunity to work with hardware in the second term. You will learn practical application of robotics concepts like perception, localization, path planning and controls using the languages and frameworks that are in demand in the industry (Python, C++, ROS, Gazebo).</p>">
              <p>Our goal with this program is to equip you with the most valuable skills in this field; the skills top companies are looking for as they search for the next generation of robotics talent. Enter the search terms Robotics Engineer in <a href="https://www.glassdoor.com/index.htm" target="_blank">Glassdoor</a>, <a href="https://www.indeed.com/" target="_blank">Indeed</a>, or any other major job search engine, and youll find thousands of openings all over the world in a diversity of industries. To ensure youre well-prepared to meet this demand, this program will focus on the software behind robotics systems, while also providing you the opportunity to work with hardware in the second term. You will learn practical application of robotics concepts like perception, localization, path planning and controls using the languages and frameworks that are in demand in the industry (Python, C++, ROS, Gazebo).</p>
             </div> </li>
            <li _ngcontent-c37=""> <h6 _ngcontent-c37="" class="h4">What are the prerequisites for this program?</h6> 
             <!---->
             <div _ngcontent-c37="" class="answer-content" innerhtml="<p>Students should have the following skills coming into the program:</p><ul><li><p>Linear algebra and calculus.</p></li><li><p>Probability and statistics.</p></li><li><p>Basic physics (Newtonian Mechanics)</p></li><li><p>Unix / Linux command line familiarity</p></li><li><p>Intermediate-level programming experience in Python or similar language</p></li><li><p>ROS, C++ and machine learning experience are helpful but not required.</p></li></ul><p>Looking to refresh your skills or prepare now? Get started with the following resources:</p><ul><li><p><a href=&quot;/course/nd009&quot; rel=&quot;nofollow&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;>Machine Learning Engineer Nanodegree &amp;#8212; Udacity</a></p></li><li><a href=&quot;/course/cs373&quot; rel=&quot;nofollow&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;>AI for Robotics</a><p></p></li><li><p><a href=&quot;/course/ud036&quot; rel=&quot;nofollow&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;>Programming Foundations with Python &amp;#8212; Udacity</a></p></li><li><p><a href=&quot;https://www.sololearn.com/Course/CPlusPlus/&quot; rel=&quot;nofollow&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;>C++ tutorial by Sololearn</a></p></li><li><p><a href=&quot;/course/ud595&quot; rel=&quot;nofollow&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;>Linux Command Line Basics</a></p></li><li><p><a href=&quot;https://www.khanacademy.org/math/statistics-probability&quot; rel=&quot;nofollow&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;>Statistics and Probability &amp;#8212; Khan Academy</a></p></li><li><p><a href=&quot;https://www.khanacademy.org/math/linear-algebra&quot; rel=&quot;nofollow&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;>Linear Algebra &amp;#8212; Khan Academy</a></p></li><li><p><a href=&quot;https://www.khanacademy.org/math/multivariable-calculus&quot; rel=&quot;nofollow&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;>Multivariable Calculus &amp;#8212; Khan Academy</a></p></li><li><p><a href=&quot;http://wiki.ros.org/ROS/Tutorials&quot; rel=&quot;nofollow&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;>ROS Tutorials</a></p></li></ul>">
              <p>Students should have the following skills coming into the program:</p>
              <ul>
               <li><p>Linear algebra and calculus.</p></li>
               <li><p>Probability and statistics.</p></li>
               <li><p>Basic physics (Newtonian Mechanics)</p></li>
               <li><p>Unix / Linux command line familiarity</p></li>
               <li><p>Intermediate-level programming experience in Python or similar language</p></li>
               <li><p>ROS, C++ and machine learning experience are helpful but not required.</p></li>
              </ul>
              <p>Looking to refresh your skills or prepare now? Get started with the following resources:</p>
              <ul>

               <li><p><a href="https://www.sololearn.com/Course/CPlusPlus/" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">C++ tutorial by Sololearn</a></p></li>
               <li><p><a href="/course/ud595" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">Linux Command Line Basics</a></p></li>
               <li><p><a href="https://www.khanacademy.org/math/statistics-probability" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">Statistics and Probability  Khan Academy</a></p></li>

               <li><p><a href="http://wiki.ros.org/ROS/Tutorials" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">ROS Tutorials</a></p></li>
              </ul>
             </div> </li>
            <li _ngcontent-c37=""> <h6 _ngcontent-c37="" class="h4">What frameworks/languages/technologies will this program teach?</h6> 
             <!---->
             <div _ngcontent-c37="" class="answer-content" innerhtml="<p>You will learn practical application of robotics concepts like perception, localization, path planning and controls using the languages and frameworks that are in demand in the industry (Python, C++, ROS, Gazebo)</p>">
              <p>You will learn practical application of robotics concepts like perception, localization, path planning and controls using the languages and frameworks that are in demand in the industry (Python, C++, ROS, Gazebo)</p>
             </div> </li>
            <li _ngcontent-c37=""> <h6 _ngcontent-c37="" class="h4">Do I need any special equipment to take this program?</h6> 
             <!---->
             <div _ngcontent-c37="" class="answer-content" innerhtml="<p>No. Nothing is required to complete the program except for a model of computer capable of running our programs and an internet connection. The minimum computational prerequisite requirements for this Nanodegree Program are the following:</p><ul><li><p>4GB RAM</p></li><li><p>Quad-Core i5 processor or equivalent</p></li><li><p>50GB free HDD space</p></li><li><p>WiFi capability (802.11x)</p></li></ul>">
              <p>No. Nothing is required to complete the program except for a model of computer capable of running our programs and an internet connection. The minimum computational prerequisite requirements for this Nanodegree Program are the following:</p>
              <ul>
               <li><p>4GB RAM</p></li>
               <li><p>Quad-Core i5 processor or equivalent</p></li>
               <li><p>50GB free HDD space</p></li>
               <li><p>WiFi capability (802.11x)</p></li>
              </ul>
             </div> </li>
            <li _ngcontent-c37=""> <h6 _ngcontent-c37="" class="h4">Is there a hardware component to the program?</h6> 
             <!---->
             <div _ngcontent-c37="" class="answer-content" innerhtml="<p>In the second term, in addition to offering students the continued opportunity to work in a software simulation environment, but we will also provide certain hardware equipment to those students able to receive shipments from our global shipping partner.</p>">
              <p>In the second term, in addition to offering students the continued opportunity to work in a software simulation environment, but we will also provide certain hardware equipment to those students able to receive shipments from our global shipping partner.</p>
             </div> </li>
            <li _ngcontent-c37=""> <h6 _ngcontent-c37="" class="h4">What if I cannot receive equipment shipments? Does that impact my ability to successfully complete the program?</h6> 
             <!---->
             <div _ngcontent-c37="" class="answer-content" innerhtml="<p>It does not. The skills and concepts we teach can all be mastered in the simulation environment, and regardless of whether you work on hardware or not, you will still be able to successfully graduate from the program.</p>">
              <p>It does not. The skills and concepts we teach can all be mastered in the simulation environment, and regardless of whether you work on hardware or not, you will still be able to successfully graduate from the program.</p>
             </div> </li>
            <li _ngcontent-c37=""> <h6 _ngcontent-c37="" class="h4">Are there additional costs associated with the hardware option?</h6> 
             <!---->
             <div _ngcontent-c37="" class="answer-content" innerhtml="<p>Udacity will cover the cost of the hardware that will be used in the program. Shipping costs and applicable taxes will be the responsibility of the student.</p>">
              <p>Udacity will cover the cost of the hardware that will be used in the program. Shipping costs and applicable taxes will be the responsibility of the student.</p>
             </div> </li>
            <li _ngcontent-c37=""> <h6 _ngcontent-c37="" class="h4">Are there additional advanced hardware requirements for the program?</h6> 
             <!---->
             <div _ngcontent-c37="" class="answer-content" innerhtml="<p>No. You may opt to purchase or use additional hardware at your option and certain content may reference such opportunities to learn about advance hardware, but you are not required to do so to successfully graduate from this program.</p>">
              <p>No. You may opt to purchase or use additional hardware at your option and certain content may reference such opportunities to learn about advance hardware, but you are not required to do so to successfully graduate from this program.</p>
             </div> </li>
            <li _ngcontent-c37=""> <h6 _ngcontent-c37="" class="h4">Can you tell me more about the balance of software and hardware in this program?</h6> 
             <!---->
             <div _ngcontent-c37="" class="answer-content" innerhtml="<p>In Term One, you&amp;#8217;ll establish the necessary foundation to tackle a wide range of challenges in robotics, and you&amp;#8217;ll master core skills and concepts as you work in the simulation environment. In Term Two, more advanced techniques and their implementations will be covered, and the hardware option will be introduced. For those students who receive the hardware equipment, you&amp;#8217;ll experience implementing these new techniques on the hardware platform; students continuing on with the simulation environment will master these same cutting-edge skills in simulation.</p>">
              <p>In Term One, youll establish the necessary foundation to tackle a wide range of challenges in robotics, and youll master core skills and concepts as you work in the simulation environment. In Term Two, more advanced techniques and their implementations will be covered, and the hardware option will be introduced. For those students who receive the hardware equipment, youll experience implementing these new techniques on the hardware platform; students continuing on with the simulation environment will master these same cutting-edge skills in simulation.</p>
             </div> </li>
            <li _ngcontent-c37=""> <h6 _ngcontent-c37="" class="h4">When do we learn details about the hardware being offered?</h6> 
             <!---->
             <div _ngcontent-c37="" class="answer-content" innerhtml="<p>All enrolled students receive details about second term curriculum midway through the first term. These details will include specifics about the opportunity to work on a robotics hardware platform, and will cover logistics related to this opportunity.</p>">
              <p>All enrolled students receive details about second term curriculum midway through the first term. These details will include specifics about the opportunity to work on a robotics hardware platform, and will cover logistics related to this opportunity.</p>
             </div> </li>
            <li _ngcontent-c37=""> <h6 _ngcontent-c37="" class="h4">Whats the job market like for Robotics Software Developers?</h6> 
             <!---->
             <div _ngcontent-c37="" class="answer-content" innerhtml="<p>Demand is strong for engineers across all aspects of robotics.               <p>Demand is strong for engineers across all aspects of robotics. Enter the search terms Robotics Engineer in <a href="https://www.glassdoor.com/index.htm" target="_blank">Glassdoor</a>, <a href="https://www.indeed.com/" target="_blank">Indeed</a>, or any other major job search engine and youll find thousands of openings all over the world in a diversity of industries.</p>
             </div> </li>
            <li _ngcontent-c37=""> <h6 _ngcontent-c37="" class="h4">How Can I Connect with the Udacity Robotics Community?</h6> 
             <!---->
             <div _ngcontent-c37="" class="answer-content" innerhtml="<p>To stay informed of the latest program news, events, and to connect with others passionate about Robotics, join the Udacity Robotics Slack Community <a href=&quot;https://robotics.udacity.com/&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;>here</a>.</p>">
              <p>To stay informed of the latest program news, events, and to connect with others passionate about Robotics, join the Udacity Robotics Slack Community <a href="https://robotics.udacity.com/" target="_blank">here</a>.</p>
             </div> </li>

           <ul _ngcontent-c37="" class="faq__list"> 
            <!---->
            <h5 _ngcontent-c37="" class="h3">Application Process</h5> 
            <!---->
            <li _ngcontent-c37=""> <h6 _ngcontent-c37="" class="h4">Why is there an application process for the Robotics Nanodegree?</h6> 
             <!---->
             <div _ngcontent-c37="" class="answer-content" innerhtml="<p>Given the specialized nature of this curriculum, it&amp;#8217;s important that enrolled students have the required knowledge, skills, and experience in advance. This process allows us to assess each applicant's qualifications, and either accept them to the program, or make recommendations for courses that will help them meet the prerequisites so they can truly succeed in the program.</p>">
              <p>Given the specialized nature of this curriculum, its important that enrolled students have the required knowledge, skills, and experience in advance. This process allows us to assess each applicant's qualifications, and either accept them to the program, or make recommendations for courses that will help them meet the prerequisites so they can truly succeed in the program.</p>
             </div> </li>
            <li _ngcontent-c37=""> <h6 _ngcontent-c37="" class="h4">What are the application selection criteria? Do I need to have specific programming experience?</h6> 
             <!---->
             <div _ngcontent-c37="" class="answer-content" innerhtml="<p>You must have previous knowledge of math (calculus, linear algebra, statistics) and basic physics. You must also have intermediate-level programming experience in Python or similar language.  Experience with ROS, C++ and machine learning experience are helpful but not required.</p>">
              <p>You must have previous knowledge of math (calculus, linear algebra, statistics) and basic physics. You must also have intermediate-level programming experience in Python or similar language. Experience with ROS, C++ and machine learning experience are helpful but not required.</p>
             </div> </li>

             <!---->

Selected applicants will be notified by June 29th with a link to the necessary enrollment details, and will have 5 days to enroll and submit their tuition payment.</p>">
              <p>Applications will open on May 3rd and be accepted through June 22nd. Selected applicants will be notified by June 29th with a link to the necessary enrollment details, and will have 5 days to enroll and submit their tuition payment.</p>

             </div> </li>
            <li _ngcontent-c37=""> <h6 _ngcontent-c37="" class="h4">Am I required to pay for both terms up front?</h6> 
             <!---->

             <!---->

            <h5 _ngcontent-c37="" class="h3">Program Structure</h5> 
            <!---->
            <li _ngcontent-c37=""> <h6 _ngcontent-c37="" class="h4">When does the first cohort start and end?</h6> 
             <!---->
             <div _ngcontent-c37="" class="answer-content" innerhtml="<p>The first cohort of students will start their first term on May 24, 2017 and complete the term 12 weeks later.</p>">
              <p>The first cohort of students will start their first term on May 24, 2017 and complete the term 12 weeks later.</p>
             </div> </li>
            <li _ngcontent-c37=""> <h6 _ngcontent-c37="" class="h4">How is this Nanodegree program structured?</h6> 
             <!---->
             <div _ngcontent-c37="" class="answer-content" innerhtml="<p>The program is comprised of 2 terms (3 months each) with fixed start and end dates. Students must successfully complete all assigned projects by the end date for each term to graduate. There are 3-4 projects per term, which give you an opportunity to apply the skills you&amp;#8217;ve learned in the lessons.  Each project must be submitted for review by one of the expert project reviewers in the Udacity Robotics network.  Your reviewer will give you detailed feedback on your work and let you know where your project needs improvement if necessary. You may submit each project as many times as you like. </p>">
              <p>The program is comprised of 2 terms (3 months each) with fixed start and end dates. Students must successfully complete all assigned projects by the end date for each term to graduate. There are 3-4 projects per term, which give you an opportunity to apply the skills youve learned in the lessons. Each project must be submitted for review by one of the expert project reviewers in the Udacity Robotics network. Your reviewer will give you detailed feedback on your work and let you know where your project needs improvement if necessary. You may submit each project as many times as you like. </p>
             </div> </li>
            <li _ngcontent-c37=""> <h6 _ngcontent-c37="" class="h4">Will there be a Nanodegree Plus version of this program, with the job guarantee?</h6> 
             <!---->

We work directly with recruiters and hiring managers at each company to get our students fast-tracked into open opportunities.</p>">
              <p>We are not offering Nanodegree Plus for this program. However, our current global hiring partnerswhich include Bosch, iRobot, Lockheed Martin, X, and moreprovide Udacity students direct and preferential exposure to new jobs. We work directly with recruiters and hiring managers at each company to get our students fast-tracked into open opportunities.</p>
             </div> </li>

             <!---->
             <div _ngcontent-c37="" class="answer-content" innerhtml="<p>Due to the singular nature of&amp;#8212;and requirements for&amp;#8212;this curriculum, we will not be supporting Connect sessions for the Robotics Nanodegree program. While students of this program are welcome to attend Connect sessions, we will not provide curriculum support at the sessions, nor will there be session leads onsite who are equipped to provide specific program guidance and input.</p>">
              <p>Due to the singular nature ofand requirements forthis curriculum, we will not be supporting Connect sessions for the Robotics Nanodegree program. While students of this program are welcome to attend Connect sessions, we will not provide curriculum support at the sessions, nor will there be session leads onsite who are equipped to provide specific program guidance and input.</p>
             </div> </li>

             <!---->
             <div _ngcontent-c37="" class="answer-content" innerhtml="<p>The fixed-term nature of the program, and the need for maintaining a consistent and stable student body throughout, doesn&amp;#8217;t allow for offering the option to pause your studies.</p>">
              <p>The fixed-term nature of the program, and the need for maintaining a consistent and stable student body throughout, doesnt allow for offering the option to pause your studies.</p>
             </div> </li>
            <li _ngcontent-c37=""> <h6 _ngcontent-c37="" class="h4">Is this program self-paced?</h6> 
             <!---->
             <div _ngcontent-c37="" class="answer-content" innerhtml="<p>The start and end dates of each term are fixed, and you must complete all assigned projects by the end dates, so to that extent, the answer is &amp;#8220;no, it is not self-paced.&amp;#8221; You must complete the program within a fixed time period. However, projects may be submitted at any time during the term, and individual project deadlines are recommendations, not requirements. So within the boundaries of a given term, there is some opportunity to work at your own pace. But you should plan to follow our recommended timeline, as this will best enable you to keep pace with your peers, and complete the program on time.</p>">
              <p>The start and end dates of each term are fixed, and you must complete all assigned projects by the end dates, so to that extent, the answer is no, it is not self-paced. You must complete the program within a fixed time period. However, projects may be submitted at any time during the term, and individual project deadlines are recommendations, not requirements. So within the boundaries of a given term, there is some opportunity to work at your own pace. But you should plan to follow our recommended timeline, as this will best enable you to keep pace with your peers, and complete the program on time.</p>
             </div> </li> 
           </ul>

            <!---->
            <h5 _ngcontent-c37="" class="h3">Deadline Policy</h5> 
            <!---->
            <li _ngcontent-c37=""> <h6 _ngcontent-c37="" class="h4"></h6> 
             <!---->
             <div _ngcontent-c37="" class="answer-content" innerhtml="<p>When we use the term &amp;#34;deadline&amp;#34; with regards to Nanodegree Program projects, we use it in one of two ways:</p><ul><li><p>To mean a final deadline for submitting all projects</p></li><li><p>To refer to ongoing suggested deadlines for individual projects</p></li></ul><p>It is very important to understand the distinctions between the two, as your progress in the program is measured against the deadlines we've established. Please see below for an explanation of what each usage means.</p>">
              <p>When we use the term "deadline" with regards to Nanodegree Program projects, we use it in one of two ways:</p>
              <ul>
               <li><p>To mean a final deadline for submitting all projects</p></li>
               <li><p>To refer to ongoing suggested deadlines for individual projects</p></li>
              </ul>
              <p>It is very important to understand the distinctions between the two, as your progress in the program is measured against the deadlines we've established. Please see below for an explanation of what each usage means.</p>
             </div> </li>
            <li _ngcontent-c37=""> <h6 _ngcontent-c37="" class="h4">A final deadline for submitting all projects</h6> 
             <!---->
             <div _ngcontent-c37="" class="answer-content" innerhtml="<p>In order to graduate a term, you must submit all projects by the last day of the term and pass all projects once they are reviewed by a Udacity Reviewer (the review may take place after the last day of the term). Passing a project means a Udacity Reviewer has marked a project as &amp;#34;Meets Specifications.&amp;#34;</p><p>If you do not submit all projects by the end of the term and also pass all projects once they are reviewed: You will receive a 4-week extension to complete any outstanding projects. You will only receive this extension a maximum of once. Once you submit and pass all projects, you can enroll in the next term, which will potentially be with a later class. If you do not submit and pass all projects within the 4-week extension, you will be removed from the program.</p>">
              <p>In order to graduate a term, you must submit all projects by the last day of the term and pass all projects once they are reviewed by a Udacity Reviewer (the review may take place after the last day of the term). Passing a project means a Udacity Reviewer has marked a project as "Meets Specifications."</p>
              <p>If you do not submit all projects by the end of the term and also pass all projects once they are reviewed: You will receive a 4-week extension to complete any outstanding projects. You will only receive this extension a maximum of once. Once you submit and pass all projects, you can enroll in the next term, which will potentially be with a later class. If you do not submit and pass all projects within the 4-week extension, you will be removed from the program.</p>
             </div> </li>
            <li _ngcontent-c37=""> <h6 _ngcontent-c37="" class="h4">Ongoing suggested deadlines for individual projects</h6> 
             <!---->
             <div _ngcontent-c37="" class="answer-content" innerhtml="<p>The deadlines you see in your classroom are suggestions for when you should ideally pass each project. They are meant to help keep you on track so that you maintain an appropriate pace throughout the program&amp;#8211;one that will see you graduate on time!</p><p>Please note that you can submit your project as many times as you need to. There are no penalties if you miss these deadlines. However, you will be at risk of not passing all projects on time if you miss these deadlines, and fall behind, so it is a recommended best practice to try and meet each suggested deadline.</p>">
              <p>The deadlines you see in your classroom are suggestions for when you should ideally pass each project. They are meant to help keep you on track so that you maintain an appropriate pace throughout the programone that will see you graduate on time!</p>
              <p>Please note that you can submit your project as many times as you need to. There are no penalties if you miss these deadlines. However, you will be at risk of not passing all projects on time if you miss these deadlines, and fall behind, so it is a recommended best practice to try and meet each suggested deadline.</p>
             </div> </li> 
           </ul>
